 rajd samarthakon kii fouj haathon main laathiyaan or bent liye hue thi
 These people were seen burning tires and bamboo on the busiest routes of the capital
 adhikariyon ne kaha ki samarthakon ne patna vishvavidhyalay ke collejon kii kakshaen baadhit kin or collejon ko jabaran band karaayaa
 Chief Public Relations Officer of East Central Railway, Arvind Kumar Rajak said, there are reports of bandh supporters disrupting rail services at many places in the state

 The RJD has called for this bandh to bolster its demand for early release of caste-based census data conducted by the Center
 haalanki rajd pramukh lalu prasad yadav ne kuch din pehle bihar band kaa aahvaan karte hue apane samarthakon se kaha tha ki vah is band ko lagu karte samay rail sevaayen baadhit na karen
 But it seems that his appeal had no effect on the supporters
 band ko sattadhari jadyu or sapa kaa bhi samarthan he, kyonki unke kaaryakartaaon ko bhi rajya kii rajdhani ke kuch kshetron main ise lagu karte hue dekha gaya
